Sun Hanbing's Lecture Yesterday: How to Study Political Science 168

Yesterday marked the eighth day of the National Reading Movement Conference, organized by the China Cultural Construction Association. The association specially invited Sun Hanbing to lecture on how to study political science. The following is a record of his speech:

Subject and Content

Ladies and gentlemen, I am honored to be invited by the China Cultural Construction Association to give this lecture on how to study political science. I will now talk about it in simple terms. There is an old Chinese saying, "If you are not in the position, do not plan its affairs." In fact, these two sentences are not very suitable for present-day China. If every citizen is so passive and irresponsible towards national politics, how can national politics get on the right track? Today's China needs citizens who are responsible and proactive towards national affairs. They need to have a sense of responsibility and a proactive attitude towards national affairs. Then, we, as general citizens, must have sufficient political knowledge to understand and study the national situation and the world's trends. Therefore, studying politics can be said to be a requirement for modern people and a common-sense that citizens should possess. As for the subject and content of studying political science, what exactly is it? To understand the meaning of the two words "politics," it refers to the coercive dominance or ruling relationship among human beings. In every society, the materially or intellectually stronger always want the weaker to obey their will and be subject to their power. The strong rule the people, and the weak are ruled by the people. The political life of mankind begins with the division between rulers and the ruled. This is an ironclad fact that we cannot deny. When necessary, the ruler can use their supreme power to enforce their policies and achieve their goals through methods such as imprisonment, exile, and execution. They can be absolutely free from the control of others. However, rulers cannot abuse their power and are subject to various restrictions imposed by the customs, habits, and morals of the time. In a given society, an individual or a group of people uses their power to rule over the rest of the people, which we collectively call politics. Therefore, political science is the social science that studies the coercive ruling or dominating relationships among human beings. The content of political science can be roughly divided into three types: political science, political philosophy, and political technology. Political science studies the political life of mankind in the past and present, and finds out the causal relationships and the laws of change. Principles of political science, political history, and the history of political thought all belong to political science. Political philosophy, on the other hand, is based on value judgments and comprehensively explores the pure theoretical foundations and ultimate nature of political phenomena. In ordinary political science books, scientific research and philosophical arguments are often mixed together, but in theory, there is a big difference between the two. Political technology studies the practical organization and governance of public affairs, as well as methods for achieving specific goals. For example, public administration and political policy science belong to this category. Therefore, specifically speaking, the questions that political science seeks to answer can be briefly listed as follows: What are the interrelationships of human political life? What exactly is the organization of human political life called the state? Do all human beings in the world, regardless of race, belief, or cultural level, have various similar political organizations? If so, what is the reason for the universal existence of such political organizations? The occurrence and evolution of the state, the relationship between the ruler and the ruled, the organization of the government and its duties, etc., are all issues that those who study politics must study.

Research Methods

The general research method is none other than the scientific method. The so-called scientific method is deduction and induction. Ordinary people often regard these two methods as incompatible, but this is a misconception. It should be known that there is actually only one method of research, which is divided into three steps: first, the observation of facts; second, the establishment of hypotheses; and third, the mutual verification of the observed facts and the established hypotheses to see if they are consistent. However, this is a general research method that can be applied to social sciences, natural sciences, and even methods of conduct. However, the study of specialized subjects should have specialized methods, the so-called technical methods. The specialized methods of studying political science are now described as follows: The first is the method of observation. Observation is the foundation of scientific research. It is to observe and investigate the actual situation of things from the standpoint of an observer and with an objective attitude, record what is observed, and then carry out various sorting and analysis. The second is the method of statistics, which is the method of collecting, analyzing, and helping to explain social facts in the form of quantities. Although the statistical method cannot directly discover the causal relationship of political or social phenomena for us, it expresses complex social and political phenomena in extremely simple and easy-to-understand numerical forms, which is indeed an important and good tool for researchers of social science. The third is the method of comparison, which is to study the various political and social systems or lives of the present or the past, compare their similarities and differences, in order to obtain ordinary and definite conclusions. The fourth is the historical method, which is to search for materials about the facts to be studied from various historical records. The historical method can not only make me know the origin and the background of the development of a system, but also provide us with many reference materials to explain the phenomenon of the present society. The methods of studying political science are probably as described above. In short, the methods of research vary according to the difference of the subject matter, and are constantly changing with the wisdom and spirit of human research.

Practical Application

No matter what kind of theory, its highest value and greatest purpose lie in practice. The purpose of our studying political science is how to rationalize, beautify, and idealize the political life of mankind. Speaking of practice, we cannot but pay attention to the needs and limitations of time and space. Assuming that we forget the dominion of time and space, it is an impossible fantasy that will not work. For example, direct democracy is indeed a very good system in itself, with all people directly participating in politics, but this system is definitely not applicable to any country. For example, our China, if we now immediately implement direct democracy, I am convinced that the benefits of direct democracy will not be seen, and the abuses will be numerous. Therefore, no matter what kind of science, its highest value and greatest purpose are in practice, but as a prerequisite for practice, we cannot forget the needs and dominion of time and space. That's all.

Gathering Elites to Exert All Efforts in One Move, Yangshupu Forcefully Defeats Nanmin, Extremely Tense Situation in the Rain During the Four-Game Match, Nanmin Loses the First Two Games and Fails to Recover, Suffering a Miserable Defeat, Nanmin Team Leaves Shanghai This Morning to Return North 177

The North China Volleyball Champion Nanmin Team, this time on a difficult journey south to Tianjin, Beijing, and Shanghai, was invincible wherever it went, winning victories. After arriving in Shanghai, it first defeated Dongya and then Jiangwan. Yesterday, it met with the Yangshupu Volleyball Team at Shanghai University. The Yangshupu Volleyball Team knew in advance that Nanmin was indeed very strong, so it specially gathered elites from Shanghai University, Yinghua, Soochow, and other schools into one group, forming a strong team to give it its all. It finally defeated Nanmin, but the battle was quite arduous. The Nanmin Team was not accustomed to fighting in the heavy rain that day, and at the same time, the Yangshupu Team gathered the elites of the city to compete against it, resulting in its defeat. The situation at that time was extremely exciting and rare. The details are recorded as follows:

First Game: The battle began at four o'clock. The Yangshupu team served first. Mai Bingyao, Li Xizhao, and Huang Hanming bravely attacked. The Nanmin team cautiously defended and was not attacked. Then, the Yangshupu team's ball was too fierce, and the front row committed suicide and lost one point. Afterwards, Nanmin's Liu Zhicong worked hard and scored one point after another. Later, Yangshupu went straight to the clouds and took the lead with five to one. Nanmin quickly caught up, making it three to six. Afterwards, Yangshupu's Zheng Yiquan worked hard to advance, forming an advantage of nine to four. Nanmin launched three balls, and the momentum was fierce, increasing by three points in a row, making it seven to nine. Afterwards, through the fierce blocking of the middle row generals, it created a tie of nine to nine. Before long, Yangshupu took the lead with eleven to nine. Switching sides and fighting again, Nanmin's repeated kills were strictly prevented by the opponent, resulting in suicide, which made Yangshupu an advantage of sixteen to nine. Nanmin was not willing to be outdone, taking the lead and chasing to thirteen to sixteen. Yangshupu went straight up, and finally ended the game with twenty-one to fourteen. Yangshupu took the first game.

Second Game: After the serve, Nanmin tried to counterattack. The middle row wings succeeded one after another. Liu Zhicong in the front row also took the opportunity to block. In an instant, they led with nine to four. The two guards of Yangshupu are old hands in this area. They linked up and attacked, displaying their magical abilities, chasing to eleven to eight, only three points behind. After switching sides, Yangshupu went down in one go and took the lead with sixteen to fourteen. After entering, Nanmin once revived, calmly fighting back, and the score increased to a tie of twenty to twenty-three. Wei Dingyi took the opportunity to serve and gained two points. Yangshupu then won the second game with twenty-two to twenty.

Third Game: Nanmin had lost two games, so they embraced the ambition of breaking the cauldron and sinking the boat, and the momentum was turbulent. Although Yangshupu was an elite at the time, they sighed that heroes had no place to use their force. The two guards in the back row, Shen Erchang and Wang Dachun, provided support on the left and right, just right. The front row, Jin Adu and Liu Zhicong, had no worries, so they showed their skills, splitting and killing the ball, without missing a single one. Until after the switch of eleven to ten, Yangshupu desperately chased and took the lead with thirteen to eleven. Nanmin's attack was also fierce, and the scores went up and down, always close. Nanmin finally relied on the pressure of Jin, Liu, Feng, etc. to win back a game with twenty-two to twenty.

Fourth Game: After the start, Yangshupu scored first. Nanmin's Jin and Feng showed their magical powers, only to see them jumping up and down, tumbling and hitting, scoring three points. Yangshupu's Mai Bingyi struck with all his might, and Wei Dingyi's iron arm lifted up, accomplishing everything, taking the lead with five to three. After Nanmin won the switch from eleven to ten, Yangshupu concentrated its energy. Mai Wei killed with one block and one kill, and all returned with success. Nanmin's situation was greatly saddened by the decline of the river, and as a result, it was frustrated with a very close score of twenty-one to eighteen.

Finance: June Term Market - Margin Money Breaks 800 Yuan Mark - Overall Trend Seems to Shift with Exchange Rate Market - Initial Drop Followed by Rise, Resulting in a Relatively Stable Outcome - Gold Exchange to be Closed for Three Days Starting on the 19th 188

The gold market saw an initial drop followed by a rise yesterday. Factoring in swap transactions, the final outcome was level. The overall trend seemed to shift with the exchange rate market. With unsettled sentiments, the price once touched a low of 799 yuan. The exchange rate market tightened, resulting in a rebound of around 20 yuan. Early in the morning, overseas reports indicated that silver prices in both the UK and the US had slightly retreated, with a fall in forward silver prices in Montedeo. The exchange rate was slightly long, and the London gold price dropped by three and a half pence. People, mindful of the sharp price declines of the previous period, were generally cautious. As such, initial off-market transactions were only in the range of 18 to 19 yuan. Factoring in swap transactions, this was only slightly more stable compared to the previous closing. However, sellers continued to flock to the market, and lacking substantial support, the downward trend intensified, eventually falling back to 780 yuan. The Central Bank's published rates showed increases in both the UK and the US, with a decrease of 1.4% in the Customs Gold Unit. The standard price for margin money was lowered to 864.7 yuan. Seeing that the prices remained stable at low levels, the general sentiment was calm. Major players also showed an appetite for buying, and the price rose past the 10 yuan mark. After the opening, the exchange rate hardened due to the inability of Jewish merchant Qiao Zhifu to find a counterparty for his dumping of shillings, leading to a severe decline. However, due to aggressive buying by major players taking advantage of the low prices, and slight increases in support from banks, the market rebounded, with a price increase of almost 10 yuan. Upon learning that the HSBC bank had posted its rates, with an increase of half a penny for the British pound and one yuan for the US dollar, the upward momentum was hindered and the price retreated within the 10 yuan range. Sassoon and China Merchants Bank aggressively dumped shillings, causing the domestic market to become unusually tight, exacerbating the selling pressure and leading to a collapse of long positions. Amidst occasional short covering, supply temporarily exceeded demand, breaking the 800 yuan mark. Major players took the opportunity to cover their positions at the low prices, and banks also stepped in to provide support. As the exchange rate market gradually tightened, prices gradually rose. Although not very impactful, news from the Associated Press that the Hong Kong government was considering banning silver exports did slightly improve sentiment, pushing the price above the 10 yuan mark. Sellers took advantage of the high prices to continue selling, and Guangdong traders re-emerged, eventually pushing the price back within the 10 yuan range. At noon, with an unsettled overall trend, the market bottomed out and then rebounded. Later in the market, with reports of small increases in Indian silver prices of 6, 7, and 10 annas, off-market prices immediately rose above the 10 yuan mark. After the opening, banks slightly sold on the high prices, and Guangdong traders continued to sell, causing the price to retreat within the 10 yuan range once again. The Daily Bank worked hard to provide support, but with a shortage of shillings, the exchange rate market tightened, and prices gradually rebounded. However, major short players aggressively added to their positions on the high prices, leading to many sell orders. Banks maintained a healthy appetite for buying, resulting in a surge of buyers. Cotton Yarn: Shanghai Inventory Gradually Decreases; Yarn Market Decline Difficult 193

The yarn market is mediocre, and the overall trend is wavering again. However, general retail investors tend to short sell and are bearish due to the instability of the gold market and the extension of exchange rates. However, a certain major player's long position remains unchanged, with no intention of exiting the market. Therefore, although the atmosphere is not good, there is a lack of new sellers, mainly because the yarn inventory in Shanghai is decreasing day by day, allowing the market to maintain itself for a while.

Record of Shorting Current Month Yarn

The yarn forward market opened with each month showing a state of uncertainty. Transactions in the middle were sparse, with most holding a wait-and-see attitude. Overseas cotton markets continued to rise, while the gold market fell. The opening prices for each month were similar to the previous day. By the second or third bidding round, it was heard that margin calls caused a sudden surge in prices, and a slight bullish trend emerged. As a result, the closing prices for each month were down 1.2 to 4 jiao compared to the previous day's closing price. Grains: Flour and Wheat Market Shows Improvement; Soybean Market Turns Dull 197

The flour market was flat and stagnant yesterday. The quoted prices for foreign wheat were down 0.25 to 1 jiao for Chicago and 0.1 to 2 jiao for Canadian wheat. At the opening, due to the sharp increase in exchange rates, people inside and outside the industry were inevitably apprehensive. In addition, foreign wheat was slightly small, and the weather was still good. Prices for each month were down by 1 fen or less. However, after the second bidding round, the number of sellers decreased, and short covering increased slightly, and the market gradually improved. By the afternoon opening, it was still flat, but later, due to active short covering by customers and buyers, the market showed good signs. Although large factories were hedging, people's minds were still positive. Looking at the current situation, it is half due to the fluctuations in exchange rates and half due to the weather, which is also related. Overall, this month was better by 2.5 li, May was down by 2.5 li, June was down by 7.5 li, July was down by 5 li, August was unchanged, and September was down by 2.5 li.

The wheat market opened with favorable weather, and foreign wheat was slightly small. In the near term, due to the lack of chips, it never opened. For distant months such as July and August, the prices decreased by about 3 to 5 fen when traders from the interior slightly sold. By the afternoon opening, it was still flat, but later, due to the stabilization of the flour market and the cold and gloomy weather, people inside and outside the industry became slightly more stable. Spring and Autumn

Tidbits 199

— (No Payment Accepted)

Thinking about it, it's quite amusing to be alive. In the morning, you get up and put on clothes. After putting on clothes, you eat. After eating, you excrete. At night, you sleep. You perform the same old routine day after day until you die. Whether you are rich or poor, you can't escape this monotonous cycle.

Before entering society, I thought it would be interesting. But after entering society, I regretted coming here. It's like people who haven't married see others getting married and feel eager, wanting to find someone to marry immediately. But after actually getting married, they realize it's not a big deal. And then having children makes things even worse. When bored, they reminisce about the joys of being single and find it quite appealing. (No Payment Accepted)

Cheap 200

— Lán Shān

"Cheap" is a term used in buying and selling, meaning it's beneficial and harmless to one's own economic position. It's something that you and I both want to take advantage of.

Who doesn't like to buy cheap goods? Merchants, catering to this universal customer psychology, engage in cutthroat competition to put on their main act. Company A offers to give away four feet of silk for every foot purchased, attracting customers and wearing out their doorsteps. Company B, seeing this with envy, also launches a promotion offering seven feet for every foot purchased, sacrificing their profits to the extreme, trying to lure back lost customers from elsewhere with their invisible, alluring giant hand—cheapness. This is undoubtedly extremely cheap for the buyer, but have we ever seen the faces of those shareholders who are secretly worrying about "losing their capital"?

Also, when the maids and older sisters in the vegetable market buy entire baskets of green vegetables from the rural people for just a few copper coins, do they know that this is "rural bankruptcy"?

Some people praise others for buying an extremely cheap item, but do you know how many times it fails when they use it? And the short lifespan of the item? Thus, before the call for "cheapness" is finished, sighs of "being fooled" and curses follow.

From this, we can see that "cheapness" is one-sided and cannot be perfect for both sides. When one side is cheap, the other side always suffers a loss. This is a natural principle.

Taking advantage of cheapness is what everyone wants, but there must be a limit. You must not imitate that fool who, after marrying his wife for five months, started raising a baby, yet told everyone that it was cheap!

Mr. Shen 201

— Chén Jǐngyú

Mr. Shen is a friend who is completely foolish. Therefore, the things he does often have inconceivable ideas and novel tricks.

He was originally wealthy and often feared being targeted by bandits, so he racked his brains to come up with a "substituting a plum tree for a peach tree" method. He immediately bought a lot of thick paper and bound them into stacks of thirty to fifty sheets each, cutting them to the size of one-yuan, five-yuan, and ten-yuan banknotes from various banks. He then placed a real banknote on top and tied them up one by one with rope. The edges were then stained with dirty water to make them look like old banknotes. Then, he stored the stacks in a safe, preparing for emergencies. He boasted that it was an ingenious plan, even if Zhuge Liang were resurrected, he couldn't do better.

Opium was his only vice. He had to smoke a few puffs every day. However, he found it inconvenient to keep going to opium dens. So, he bought opium and asked someone to cook it for him, but he was troubled by the lack of ashes. Because cooking opium without ashes made the finished product not only of poor quality but also bland and tasteless. He pondered for a while, then turned around and went in. After a while, he happily came out carrying a piece of paper, exclaiming, "I have ashes!" In reality, this so-called ash was like a piece of burnt charcoal, made by roasting opium on the fire. When asked, "Why don't you just cook it all into opium paste? Why waste it?" He replied, "Then there would be no ashes!" The person was dumbfounded!

Recently, he suddenly thought of quitting opium, so he flipped through a copy of "Compendium of Materia Medica" and selected several medicines to soothe the stomach and intestines, which he boiled into a paste and drank with water. He thought that quitting opium was about promoting diarrhea. Once he had a bowel movement, the opium residue in his abdomen would definitely be removed completely, and his opium addiction would disappear without a trace! Unexpectedly, after taking the medicine, he had uncontrollable diarrhea like a burst Yellow River, almost unable to stand it. Fortunately, he still used opium to treat himself, and he managed to turn danger into safety. From then on, his addiction actually deepened!

"Exotic Flair" 202

— Jiāng Mǐ

Wild Cries 203

— Zǐwēi

Fine rain drizzling, hastening the growth of new green leaves on the tree tops. The fragrant grass is a stretch of emerald green, with no end in sight. The spring countryside scenery has taken on a new vigor.

On Qingming morning, a middle-aged couple held a bunch of fresh flowers, walking through the wheat fields, arriving at a grave, inserting the flowers at the head of the tomb, lingering and unwilling to leave quickly. After their sorrow, sighs were frequently heard. Suddenly, the wife looked into the distance, seeing an old woman holding paper money, pacing on the side of the road, appearing as if she was lost. Suddenly, she also took the road forward. Recognizing her after close examination, she urgently pulled at her husband's sleeve and said, "Let's leave. That woman is coming." In hesitation, the old woman arrived, with a pale face, seeming to nod her head, but not speaking. She sidled her body toward the front of the grave. At first she was only sobbing, and then she began to wail loudly. Her voice could be heard far and near, overwhelmingly mournful. The husband was also moved to tears. The wife revealed an impatient look and said: "Let's go, let's go. I shall go ahead." The husband did not heed her, and instead assisted the old woman to rise, saying: "Don't be so sad." The old woman cried even harder. After a while, her voice was hoarse and exhausted. Only then did she rise to burn the paper money. The remaining sorrow was not yet extinguished. At this time, the wife who had come first was already walking away in anger. The man could not bear to leave, repeatedly comforting the old woman, saying: "The deceased has passed, and you should cherish your own body. Do not be too sad for the sake of one who had a short life." The old woman with sorrow in her heart did not listen, wiping her red eyes, hunched over and walked, and walked and turned her head back, unable to bear to part. The man followed to send her off, only parting at the crossroads.

Ten years ago, that old woman was the man's wife, raising a son, extremely intelligent. When the child was fourteen years old, he graduated from junior high school. At that time, the husband had an affair, abandoning his family and eventually divorcing. The child went with his father, often taking the opportunity to visit his mother, and comforting her by saying: "Mother, do not be sad. When your son is able to stand on his own someday, he will welcome you to live with him." The wife supported herself with handicraft work. Several years passed, and the son got a job at a certain factory. Just when he was planning to save money to start a family, the January 28th Incident suddenly broke out. Enraged by the enemy's unreasonableness, he joined the volunteer army to participate in the war, and unfortunately died from a bullet wound. After the war, the father chose to bury him here. At first, the mother did not know of this. Later, hearing of the loss, she cried aloud, her business immediately ended. She regretted not knowing where the body was buried, searching and inquiring in all directions, but no one knew the answer. In recent years, her sorrow and depression has grown, and she has become increasingly haggard. Only then did she learn that his bones were buried in the eastern suburbs, and she came to seek the trace and cry at his grave on Qingming Day. She was even able to meet her former love rival, encountering layers of sadness, which was all the more pitiable.

Chatter

Discussing Teeth 204

— Zhu Yun

Teeth are the primary weapons for chewing food; whether food is thoroughly chewed is closely related to digestion. The soundness of teeth is linked to one's overall health, so oral hygiene and protecting teeth are important.

However, the condition of my teeth is quite tragic; most of them have problems. Some are decayed, others are broken. Though patched up here and there, these dentures are ultimately not as useful as my own teeth. They are either uncomfortable or lack strength. I can't chew hard things, and even when eating tender bamboo shoots, I must be especially careful. Otherwise, if the false teeth are jostled, a wave of sourness and numbness shoots straight to my heart, and the pain almost brings tears to my eyes.

I love to eat peanuts, but I can only watch others enjoy them, while I can only swallow my saliva, unable to enjoy the pleasure. Sometimes I buy some fruit pastries, but the crispy and delicious taste of peanuts is nowhere to be found. A person in their thirties already has blurred vision, graying hair, and missing teeth, truly becoming an old man in his youth. Thinking about it, I find it both laughable and regrettable!

The main reason for my tooth loss is that I loved eating sweets since I was a child, and my parents were not attentive to my dental hygiene. It wasn't until I was eleven or twelve, when I switched from private tutoring to elementary school, that I started brushing my teeth and rinsing my mouth. However, my teeth were already disorganized, blackened, and not very healthy. Sometimes when my teeth ached, the pain was so severe that I couldn't eat and my face was swollen, preventing me from sleeping well for days. So by the time I turned twenty, four or five teeth on both sides had already decayed, leaving many holes between the upper and lower rows of teeth.

Because a friend worked as an assistant at a dentist's office, he saw my decayed teeth and encouraged me to get gold teeth, offering a special price. Persuaded by him, I went to the dentist's office to get them fitted. Since two canine teeth on the left side were missing, I first got three teeth fitted: one was a shell attached to the adjacent tooth, one was a gold tooth, and one was a porcelain tooth. To fit them, the dentist first took a mold of my teeth with a red powder, then proceeded with the fitting. During the process, the dentist used a lathe to grind and grind my teeth, the vibrations sending waves of sourness and numbness, and the smell of burning filled my throat, making it very unpleasant.

After the teeth were fitted, my friend presented the bill, which amounted to sixteen dollars. This amount shocked me. After much negotiation, I angrily demanded that he remove the fitted teeth, and I paid a few dollars to settle the matter. However, a friend ended our friendship over this.

After this lesson, I dared not get gold teeth again, allowing my teeth to decay. However, at the end of last year, while chewing an olive, I bit down hard and broke half of my front tooth. Opening my mouth, it was unsightly with gaps everywhere, so I had to get it fixed again. So, my wife and I went to several small dental shops in Niujiaobing, and after much discussion, we had five gold teeth and one porcelain tooth fitted at the Tianji Dental Shop for a total of eight silver dollars. The price was indeed cheap, but they were not very comfortable. Opening my mouth, the gaps were no longer visible, but these forcibly fitted teeth were ultimately not practical. I deeply felt that protecting teeth is a crucial matter in life, especially one should pay attention to it in childhood!

Small Western Paradise 205

— Written by Zhang Henshui

Chapter Twelve: Ashamed of Having No Clothes, She Avoids Guests Behind Curtains; Diligently Saving Lamp Oil, He Copies Books at Dawn

The room he lived in could be considered first-class here. Yet, he left without worrying about people dirtying his bedding or stealing his belongings. So, he said to Yueying, "If you went to the front like this, I'm afraid Master Jia wouldn't let you sleep on his bed. It's rare to have this gentleman's kindness, so you should take off your wet clothes. I'll talk to Master Jia for you." Thus, Yang Huanhua went to the front to reply to Jia Duocai. Hu's wife took Yueying to Zhizhi's room. The tea server and Hu's wife were acquaintances, and Zhizhi had instructed them in person, so they decided to be kind and let them go into the room without interfering. Yueying walked into the room soaking wet. Whether she felt cold or not was not important; she only felt her upper and lower teeth chattering, fighting each other. Hu's wife felt a bit sorry for her trembling body, so she helped her unbutton her clothes and lowered Zhizhi's curtain. Yueying went inside the curtain and took off all her clothes, shoes, and socks. She unfolded the quilt and burrowed inside. Naturally, she wrapped herself tightly, but her body had been iced by rainwater for so long that she couldn't stop shivering. Hu's wife rolled up her clothes, shoes, and socks into a large bundle and said to her, "Rest comfortably in bed. I'll take these things to dry. I'll hook the door from the outside so no one will come in." (184)

Records of Lingering Fragrance 206

— Originally written by Princess Deling of the Qing Dynasty, translated by Qin Shouou

Although they were not all doing embroidery work at the same time, some might have been drafting designs, while others were matching threads. However, once a flower on a piece of satin was assigned to someone for embroidery, that person would eventually be responsible for completing it. Moreover, each piece of satin was not just for one pair of shoe uppers but often for five or six pairs together. Therefore, the top, bottom, left, and right sides of the satin were almost covered with patterns to be embroidered. Each female worker lowered her head—they had to lower their heads very low, almost pressing their eyes against the satin. Because this work was extremely delicate, they had to see clearly to avoid mistakes—and silently embroidered.

Now, let me explain their work process in more detail: First, they used white powder to outline several shoe upper shapes on the satin according to the drawn shoe patterns. They had to leave some space between each pair for cutting. Once the outlines were drawn, they started embroidering each shoe upper one by one. However, before embroidering each shoe upper, there was some preparatory work. For example, if a plum blossom was needed on a shoe upper, they would first cut out several differently shaped plum blossoms from thin white paper. Then, they would place these paper flowers on the drawn shoe upper on the satin, trying them here and there, using an artistic eye to determine their appropriate positions. Once the positions were determined, they would use silk thread to tack them down. The silk thread used at this time was usually white, and they didn't need to use many stitches, just enough to hold the paper flowers in place. (294)

Shen Bao Local Supplement

Talks

Teacher with Entourage 207

— Gang

Brothels have managers with entourages, and now schools have teachers with entourages. Truly, the tricks are new and getting stranger.

It is said that brothel managers with entourages bring one or two young ladies. The money earned by these young ladies is split between the brothel and the manager. So, these managers are very comfortable. In the afternoon or evening, they listen to storytelling in a few big theaters or play mahjong with some regular customers. Therefore, the lives of these managers are quite comfortable.

Who knew that in Shanghai, now known as the "New York of the East," there was also a teacher with an entourage in the education sector? According to yesterday's newspaper, Huang Kangsheng from Haimen used to teach in Yongkang, Zhejiang. This spring, through an introduction, he became a geography and history teacher at the Minhua Vocational Middle School on Yanping Road in Shanghai. At that time, he agreed with Principal Cai of the school that Huang could bring more than fifty students from Yongkang, and his salary would be higher than other teachers. Therefore, Cai agreed to pay Huang a monthly salary of fifty yuan, which was twenty yuan higher than other teachers.

Now, let me calculate this account for the principal. This business is indeed profitable. It is said that the school charges each student sixty yuan per semester for tuition, board, and miscellaneous fees. If calculated with fifty students, the school would receive three thousand yuan per semester, amounting to six thousand yuan per year. Even if the teacher is paid twenty yuan more per month, the annual cost (calculated for twelve months) would only be two hundred and forty yuan. The profit would be five thousand seven hundred and sixty yuan. Even after deducting student board and other expenses, estimated at three thousand yuan, the net profit would be more than two thousand seven hundred yuan. This business is indeed profitable.

Unfortunately, on one hand, the teacher's ability was weak, and the number of fifty students was greatly reduced. On the other hand, he had bad intentions and embezzled three hundred and fifteen yuan of tuition fees. With these two significant reductions, the principal's profit was minimal, and he naturally became furious and wanted to file a lawsuit to recover the embezzled money. This kind of scandalous history in Shanghai's education sector is truly unheard of.

However, there are many "school shops" opened in Shanghai. Some collect tuition fees but do not start classes, some only have subjects but no teachers, and some conduct trial teaching for a year before hiring. There are all kinds of tricks, so many that they cannot be written down. Then, how could a teacher with an entourage not be a money-making avenue for the school shop owner? Suppose each school had ten such teachers as Huang; at the end of the year, the results would be joyously revealed.

Flower Shop Vignette 208

— Rong

These past few evenings, when walking past the intersection of Jing'an Temple Road and Seymour Road and turning towards my residence, I have often been drawn to the vibrant and moving flower shop. Smoking a peaceful cigarette, I stood on the asphalt pavement planted with plane trees. Unexpected bursts of floral fragrance blew into my nose with the evening breeze. Turning back from the bustling road with countless lights, what caught my eye was the bright window with its thousands of reds and purples. The mottled colors were like an ancient brocade. The alluring peach blossoms, like enchanting dancers, the pale white flowers with the demeanor of philosophers, the lilacs gazing as forlornly as aggrieved women, the slender and pure redbuds, the carnations suitable for wedding banquets or hanging by purple silk curtains, and many other strange and wonderful flowers and herbs, all piled before your eyes, competing for attention. The scene truly made you forget that you were in a noisy city and instead placed you in a dazzling flower garden in April. If the window also reflected bright snow and added a few people with less of a commercial air, it would truly brew a strange and lingering mood for you.

Standing there, quietly invaded by the floral fragrance, the various elegant colors before my eyes, pale scarlet, deep purple or light purple, emerald green as fresh and moist as jadeite paired with a few delicate white dots, small blood bead-like crimson points embellishing the plain background, and yellow symbolizing noble hope, only without black and gray, such colors have no place in the realm of the blue sky. These flower branches have not been heavily trimmed, and the wild and natural charm is like that of a country girl by a bridge and flowing stream, not as hot and scorching as the women in the city, making you feel agitated, nor as coldly freezing as the old-fashioned ladies in their boudoirs, like a glass of green wine, giving you a peaceful joy as you sip and savor it. Although there is no blue wave and swallow feathers there, facing these flowers, you already know that this is spring.

Moreover, this is precisely the season of drizzling rain. Because of the rain, everything is plated with a layer of sorrowful color. The sound of cars, the voices of people, the sound of selling evening newspapers, although loud, are purely powerless at this time. The street in the evening mist, the red and green traffic lights and advertisements in the rain threads, and these flowers, when brought together, are all worth obsessing over. Inside the flower shop, it is always sunny, and it is a dreamlike sunny day in April, rich and fragrant, like a long love song. Here, there is no war, no blood, no pursuit of wealth, no sighs and tears; everything is buried in a gentle hope.

Standing outside and looking already gives one more than sensory satisfaction. If you push open the door and enter, the situation is different again. A person seems to be born into a fragrant country. The fragrant and warm air envelops your whole body, and rainbow-like colors surround you. It is as gentle as a wedding night, with an enchanting expression in front, and greasy brocade curtains and

Page 18

Elegant tassels on the side, you can't help but be intoxicated. I remember one flower shop kept a small canary. The elegant music like reed pipes directly passed through the glass window and dissipated from the green shade of the trees, harmonizing with the strange fragrance and the gorgeous colors, like a sweet dream that makes people feel lost.

When returning, I often buy a bunch or two of flowers. These flowers accompany my slender and lonely shadow as I cross the main road, walk towards the quiet residential area, and enter my residence. I put this bunch of flowers in a vase and place it next to those ancient and solemn philosophical books, just like a young maiden leaning on a kind old grandfather. When the lights are turned off, there is the fragrance of books and the fragrance of flowers in the silence. Now the flowers have begun to wither. When I am writing, I see one or two withered purple shadows, seemingly infinitely regretting their past glorious years!

On the Market Boat 209

— Tianqi

—Random Notes on Returning South—

When the east began to turn slightly white, the boatman shouted loudly, and the heavily loaded market boat shook a little and slowly drifted towards the center of the river. The river surface was covered with soft morning mist; the light green river water gently lapped against the bow in the stillness. On the south bank, under the mountains, the long calls of women summoning the ferry had already risen. Looking back, the shadows of the riverside shops in Song City gradually blurred into the smoke and mist.

Inside the empty boat canopy, there was only me, a passenger, which invisibly thickened the lonely feeling in my heart. As far as I know, ordinary market boats usually had at least twenty or thirty passengers, crowded like a beehive. Now, this unusual situation could not help but surprise me, and it quickly turned into terror. A terrifying image of boatmen plotting to kill for money, which I had seen in novels, stuck to my heart, and I regretted not taking the market boat so rashly.

There were five boatmen on board, four pushing poles at the bow, and an old man in his fifties steering the rudder. His coarse, dark skin clearly marked the decades of wind and frost he had endured. A sorrowful and helpless expression would occasionally float across his thick, dark eyebrows, invisibly intensifying his age. However, the eyes embedded under his thick eyebrows still radiated a strong and kind light, which showed that he was not discouraged by his career and that he was a good person.

My seat was in the aft cabin canopy, directly facing the old man. It was easy for us to start a conversation. After some conversation, my previous doubts completely disappeared, because he had told me that he was the owner of the boat and that we were also paternal uncle and nephew from Baima Village.

Because of our clan relationship, our conversation became much more cordial. At this time, the boat had just reached a turning dike, and the current became rapid. While he focused all his attention on the water conditions ahead, holding the rudder tightly with both hands, he panted and told me intermittently about the situation in the countryside, how difficult it was getting day by day, and how the opening of the Song County Highway had dealt a fatal blow to all the market boats.

—"The market customers, do they, who do small business also, afford to pay twice as much as the boat fare for the bus?"

—"Old nephew, you just came back, so you don't know. At first, we only lost a group of passing customers, but soon the heartless bus company said something about preferential treatment for market customers. All market customers only have to pay one-third of the bus fare. In this way, who wouldn't be happy to take the bus!"

—"Old nephew, let me say something stupid, but I think the world is only going to force us poor people to death! Is that right? Hahahaha!"

His laughter was clearly a helpless and pointless self-comfort. Just as the fate before him had cruelly shattered all his efforts, but for the sake of hunger, for the sake of the continuation and expansion of life, he still had to seek survival in despair, enduring wind and rain, and could not be discouraged and sit still and die. However, although he wanted to use laughter to cover up the pain in his heart, it was even more difficult for me to watch than to see him cry.

I did not say a word, only watched in a daze as the mountains, embankments, and forests moved slowly backwards... At this time, the sun was hanging high on the mountain peak, and the boatmen at the bow were also straining their muscles, making the tenacious cry of hauling the sea, against the current, pushing the boat towards the dangerous and difficult-to-cross Shimen shoal not far ahead...

Ba Store 210

— Jingyun

The rooster was crowing in the chicken coop behind the attap house. The sun, like a brazier, drilled out from the misty coconut groves covered with a layer of light gauze. The voices of people and animals in Bali were gradually becoming noisy and lively. At this time, Huang Shunzhi and his brother climbed out of bed. As usual, they didn't take a "cold" or "rinse," and hurriedly packed their simple luggage, ate a hasty breakfast, and bid farewell to their "boss," who was also their close clan uncle, Heqing. They left the store and took the early bus to Wanggu.

Uncle Heqing saw the two brothers out of the store, tightly holding their rough arms, spitting out sincere words like chunks of鲜red blood from the bottom of his heart:

"Shunzhi, nephew, it's not that your uncle doesn't want you two brothers to stay in the store, it's just that the store's business has become so bleak lately! If things continue like this, the future is extremely pessimistic. Maybe in another two or three months, your uncle's store will be unable to maintain itself and will close down. ... You are all young lads who can endure hardship. Staying here is not a perfect solution. You should work hard outside to have hope! ..." Uncle Heqing's heavy voice trembled, and his eyes were moist.

The Shunzhi brothers lowered their heads and responded vaguely, then walked away.

It wasn't until the shadows of the two brothers disappeared in the middle of the street that Uncle Heqing slowly walked back into his grocery store.

"If it were a few years ago, it wouldn't matter if a few more people came to live and eat in the store. At that time, the business was so prosperous! The store employed more than a dozen clerks, and it was still busy all day long, sweating all over, without a moment to spare. Who could have predicted that now, the business would become so desolate and bleak that even the problem of eating would become alarming!" Uncle Yiheqing sighed secretly in his heart. The more he thought about it, the more uneasy he felt. He felt as tired as after excessive labor. He moved his buttocks to the short stool near the counter, casually took out his pipe from the counter, filled it with tobacco, closed his eyes, and puffed away.

Uncle Heqing was an honest and loyal old man, about fifty years old. Since coming to Fanbang, he had been running this "Yuanji" grocery store in Shangba, specializing in business with the natives. At the same time, he also bought the natives' grain and transported it in large quantities to Wanggu to sell to the rice mills that husked rice. Then, he used the money he earned to purchase a large quantity of daily necessities in Wanggu and transport them to Shangba to sell to the natives.

Now the natives are not as foolish as before. They know how to do business, and the government has also opened a sales bureau in Shangba to buy the natives' grain at a fixed price and severely punish the natives for selling the grain to grain merchants at low prices. As a result, Uncle Heqing's business has been completely robbed.

Recently, the government has also sent officials to the streets to investigate the business operations and capital of various shops, saying that they will soon implement the collection of "business tax."

"In this year, business is really not easy to do! Last year, they collected some 'income tax,' and now they are coming with a 'business tax.' The market situation is getting colder and colder day by day, but the taxes are pressing people down so that they can't lift their heads!" Uncle Heqing knocked his pipe on the ground with a clatter, and muttered unhappily in his heart.

"Perhaps after Shunzhi and his brothers arrive in Wanggu, their friends will ridicule him behind his back, saying that he can't even keep his nephews, unbearable words to hear. However, who doesn't feel the difficulty of the commercial situation in this year, let alone my shop, which is already a bit precarious! ..."

When Uncle Heqing opened his eyes, which were sunken like two holes, and saw the sparse goods in the store and the silence like after noon, with not a single customer walking in, his dream of "crossing the ocean to Fanbang" and "picking up gold," which he had cherished in his heart for more than twenty years, was shattered into pieces.

Laborious Fate 211

— Ke Ming

When I arrived at Baojiakou, I unexpectedly saw that old bald mule driver again, with his head completely shaved. Everything was the same: the city wall, the river, the foot-pricking gravel on the ground. The only differences were that the old bald man's wrinkled face was even more wrinkled, withered, and shrunken than before, and those sturdy legs, which he used to boast could walk fifty li a day on the sandy roads, had also lost their vigorous posture of yesteryear. Also, that black mule with its ears perked up (we remember it was only five years old), overly exhausted but underfed, was also drooping its head, dragging its four crippled legs with a lack of energy, and burying its dull brain, incapable of contemplation, in past memories.

(But everything is still the same! The mountains, the trees, the setting sun hanging over the city walls at dusk!)

As I approached, the old bald man finally lifted his head from his empty musings. He saw me at a glance, and in his astonishment, a hint of a smile flashed like lightning across the countless wrinkles on his old face. The smile crept up the old bald man's face, which had been worn down by more than sixty years of hard living, like a ray of sunlight shining on a desolate island covered in perennial ice and snow. Though weak, perhaps it could melt a small piece of ice shavings, bearing boundless bitter cold?

"Ah ha! Fine gentleman, honored gentleman, you are so well, so content, aren't you? Ha, you certainly look much more prosperous!" His voice was hoarse and dry. He tried to make it sound more natural, younger, and more robust, but that was not an easy task.

We all had a strange feeling. Looking at the old bald man, looking at the mule, they had completely lost their former vitality. The violence of life was pushing people towards the fragile icy river of death, and now both man and beast had been pushed to the edge of the line of death.

"Old bald man, you've gotten old too."

"Ah, my gentleman: old? Yes, getting old is fine, but a laborious fate means suffering even if one doesn't get old, just like livestock. Getting old is... fine... But it's this animal that suffers!"

That's right, I remembered: the old bald man hadn't changed. He still treated that black mule like a friend.

Some time ago, we stayed in a small village near Baojiakou for a summer. We had brought some inexpensive summer medicinal materials here to trade. After settling into the inn, because the roads there were all sand, and the blazing sun made them as hot as red-hot iron, walking was not easy. So, we decided to ask the innkeeper to find a reliable mule driver and hire his mule for a month. The innkeeper called the old bald man. He said: The man is quite sturdy and reliable, the animal is strong, and the man has no family, so he can travel with guests all over the country.

That's how we started dealing with the old bald man.

Although the old bald man's sparse, almost bare temples were already gray, he was not as withered as he was now, and he walked briskly. What was particularly strange was that he had a special kindness towards his only mule. Not only would he never hit it himself, but if a guest mistreated it, the old bald man would say in a trembling voice: "Gentleman, have mercy, the livestock also have a laborious fate..."

"Old bald man, you are quite good."

"Ah, dear sir, you don't know, three years of war, my mother died, my father died, my old home is gone, my own son wandered away, and only this animal, suffering as I do, is left. People are like livestock, they also have a laborious fate..."

The three words "laborious fate" resonated with sorrowful thoughts. It seemed to hint at a person's terrible destiny, carrying a similarly vibrant life. People walk in the world, passing through mountains and seas, but some people are destined to fall into a bottomless pit of brown toil forever.

And now, it should be the turn of other people and animals to wander on the perpetually toiling brown line of death.

Travels in Johor (Continued) 212

— Hu Sizhong

We have already reached the opposite bank of the bridge: our bodies are now situated in the Malay Federation. A customs gate flashed before our eyes. The Malay police gave us a quick glance and then let us pass. As soon as we stepped onto the soil of Johor, the Johor royal palace appeared amidst the mountains. A crescent moon flag was raised above the palace, and a circle of bamboo fence surrounded the magnificent building. Johor's city then revealed smooth asphalt roads, a bustling cityscape, and the clamor of shops. Electric lights flickered, cars crowded, and the urban landscape unfolded before us.

A large group went to a restaurant to eat, as the spirit of tropical people at night is both clear and cheerful. Everyone often laughed.

After dinner, Li immediately suggested going to the Johor beach to enjoy the cool air and see the night view. So we drove the car to the beach near the iron bridge. Everyone chose chairs set up on the beach for tourists to sit down. We saw the moon hanging obliquely in the sky. A hazy moonlight shone on the sea, revealing the sea's vast and bright embrace, which was more flavorful compared to its roughness during the day. The iron bridge looked even longer at night, and the dark shadows of the forests on the opposite bank appeared even more blurred. Only a crystal-like gray-white color covered the distant area. Under the moonlight, the strings of cars and rows of electric lights appeared even more beautiful than in the evening. The sea breeze opened our hearts, and some people even lay down on the chairs.

"What a beautiful day, no wonder the King of Johor wants to become a romantic emperor!" Ming said.

"I wish I could die in the waters of the Johor Strait!" Li and Ruo said.

Everyone then stood up, preparing to push him into the sea.

After an hour or two, seeing that everyone's hearts were filled with the beautiful scenery, and the tourists on the shore were gradually thinning out, and the sound of the sea gradually rose from the low city noise, we had no choice but to leave.

The car sped across the iron bridge, and our bodies and minds were unusually comfortable and joyful. We climbed past the desolate outskirts of Lion Island again, and then entered the heart of the city from the edge. The pollution and noise of Singapore touched us again.

"Oh, how annoying Singapore is!" everyone sighed, seemingly feeling a great regret for abandoning the iron bridge and beach of Johor. (The End)

Supplement to the Shen Bao Local Edition - Film Special

Why Marjorie Evans Says She Doesn't Want to Be a Movie Star (Part 1) 216

— Xin Ni

When an actress publicly states that she doesn't want to be a star, she must already have star status. Otherwise, those words are meaningless. Marjorie Evans, one of the cast members of "Little Lord Fauntleroy," playing David Copperfield's second wife, Agnes, is the person who said these words, "I don't want to be a star." She is not just using wishful thinking to comfort herself, nor is she boasting or exaggerating. She has very good reasons and insights.

She says, "People will hear my words and say, 'Here we go again, another self-promotion,' but for me, it's a very natural and reasonable feeling. I have to explain my reasons in detail. I think Hollywood has all kinds of people, making it a good place to compare values and learn. When I ask myself whether I want my name, adorned with dazzling lights, to be displayed across the sky, larger than everyone else's name, I take a look around.

"For example, there used to be an 'It' Girl here. She was a star. From the moment she got out of bed in the morning, 'It' ruled her entire life until she went to bed. The public demanded 'It,' they paid money to see 'It,' and they had to get 'It.' I feel that 'It' is simply an inhuman life. That kind of stressful life! That 'It' Girl had to prove that she truly had 'It' not only to her audience but also to her friends, servants, journalists, company executives, directors, extras, and even the baker.

"Then look at Greta Garbo. I admire her very much and acknowledge her as a great artist. But if someone asked me to fight for her star status, I would feel it's not worth it. I think she must be very tired of those black glasses. I think she must often resent being a star because she has lost her freedom by becoming a star. She has to put on makeup wherever she goes and avoid people's eyes and ears, fearing that someone will recognize her.

"And once an actress becomes a star, her lifestyle, diet, social life, etc., must be arranged according to her star status and prestige. Even Norma Shearer, Joan Crawford, Constance Bennett, and Marlene Dietrich—who are very real women—must concentrate their energy and constantly consider their status and honor. This way, they will never have free time to relax. They must live in magnificent mansions. They must dress beautifully and fashionably. They must hire many servants. Their cars must be brand new and luxurious. They must also acquire jewelry, expensive fur coats, pedigree dogs, and have a garden, swimming pool, tennis court, and all other kinds of luxury items in their home. They are stars, and these things are what the public expects from stars.

"The four actresses mentioned above have all achieved considerable status and prestige, and it seems that they don't need to abide by that unwritten law of the film city, but they can't do it. Stars still have to compete with each other. Everything they eat, live, wear, and socialize with must be extravagant to prove and maintain their reputation. This situation is better now than before, but habits are hard to change. They still have to compare who has the most magnificent house, who has the most elegant garden, who has the most valuable car or yacht, and who has the most diamonds. This is another reason why I don't like being a star.

"If I were just a top-notch actress, not a star, I could live a simpler life. I now live with my mother and brothers in a rented house, and my life is not much different from that of an ordinary American woman. I work very hard every day, but when I'm not working, I can move freely, read books, swim, visit girlfriends, and go out and have fun. I don't have to worry about people peeking at me or bothering me, and I don't attract the attention of curious people.

"I rarely attend banquets, so I don't need many evening gowns. I haven't thought about buying a yacht. If I had one, I wouldn't know how to use it. I also don't want to customize a special car because an ordinary car is enough for my needs. I don't have to socialize with directors, flatter producers, or contact movie stars, so I don't need a garden house, swimming pool, tennis court, or many servants. But if I were a star, it wouldn't be that simple.

These are all the reasons why I don't want to be a star, but there are more reasons than just the ones mentioned above. (To be continued)

Film Review

Review of "Under Pressure" 217

Under Pressure — Grand Theater

Not long ago, I saw the trailer for "Under Pressure" at the Grand Theater. The tense scenes and excellent cinematography made me eagerly await the opening of this film. But now I am disappointed. My previous hopes have been replaced by endless emptiness. "Under Pressure" is not a successful work.

Technically speaking, I have to admit that the cinematography is still worth watching. The stark contrast of black and white contributes to the rugged atmosphere. However, the director repeatedly wasted film on road construction, always building roads and always creating contrived tension. This gives people a sluggish and monotonous feeling. I don't know if the director has much experience with underwater road construction, but I always feel that it's very different from the real situation. At the very least, he failed to use pure film techniques to convey a sense of reality. Fortunately, the worker Chuck's personality is likeable. We are very familiar with McLaglen's acting style.

The success or failure of a film cannot be judged solely by the director's or actors' skills. The script often ruins the director. Indeed, the failure of "Under Pressure" is precisely due to the writer's vulgar understanding of social reality and technically incompetent performance.

If this film has a theme at all, it is to value money as an honor, causing workers to desperately build roads and risk their lives to earn large sums of money. Can we say that this is a proper encouragement of the spirit? On the contrary, it is merely a material temptation. On the other hand, we see workers fighting over money, causing division among them. Thus, this is precisely a consistent manifestation of the American film's spirit of serving the current system.

Why Does Cecil B. DeMille Wear Riding Attire? 218

— Dong Lin

Several years ago, when the film industry was still in the silent era, Hollywood directors used to wear short shirts and riding breeches, with long boots, to the studio to work. So at that time, riding attire became like the director's uniform, just as photographers were distinguished by wearing their bird-hunting hats backwards. But with the passage of time, this custom gradually disappeared, and now it can be said that directors all wear ordinary suits to the studio.

However, there is still one person who maintains the "old days" look, and that is the great director Cecil B. DeMille!

DeMille has a dozen pairs of long boots. He never wears the same pair of boots to the studio for two consecutive days. And each pair of his long boots has different short shirts and riding breeches to match. He likes to wear khaki riding breeches and a green short shirt.

In 365 days a year, you can never see DeMille wearing a 1935-style suit in the studio! No! Regardless of whether other directors have changed their clothes, Cecil B. DeMille still wears the old riding attire, with the clatter of thick leather long boots, walking into the studio!

Many people wonder: Why does DeMille wear riding attire? The eccentric old director answered him this way: "There are two reasons: first, because I am a director. As for the second reason, it's because ordinary clothes can never withstand the intense work of being a director. And I feel very comfortable wearing this riding attire. No matter how rough you are, you don't have to worry about it breaking. So I change it every day, just because I want to feel refreshed!"

"So you don't wear it to give the actors a psychological reaction?" the reporter asked him again.

"No, no!" DeMille replied with a smile: "I believe that the actors I direct are controlled by my little bit of brains, not by this pair of long boots!"

Microphone Broadcasting 219

— Wei Bai

Dong Tianya has been extremely busy these past few days preparing the grand sets for "The Soul of the Nation" and "The Big Family." From drafting to construction to filming, he is always personally planning and directing on the side. He is considered one of the most responsible and loyal members of the film industry.

The Mingxing Bi-Weekly, I heard, has already been published and should be on sale in the next day or two. The content is written by famous figures and writers in the film industry, and it is expected to sell well.

Gao Qianping has been wearing completely black clothing from head to toe these past few days, truly resembling her nickname, "Magpie."

Shu Xiuwen is playing the role of Qiu Jin in "The Soul of the Nation." Her Japanese-style hairstyle in the makeup is quite complicated, and each time it costs one yuan and forty cents for the hairstyling fee, which is also a new record in film.

"The Season of Falling Flowers," secretly screened at the Central Theater the day before yesterday, has many poetic performances and scenes, which is another new advancement in Chinese cinema.

There is a brand new female talent named Li Qiuyin. Her face and figure are very full and beautiful. (Incomplete)

Diao Banhua, a brilliant new star of Lianhua, has left a very good impression on the Chinese people since her debut in "New Woman." Film enthusiasts have great hopes for this emerging actor.

Indeed, she is a talented person. Although she is new to the camera, her acting ability is by no means weak. She has courage, is willing to work hard, and is extremely serious, so she has already made amazing gains in "Autumn Fan Lamp" and "Wild Goose Descending on a Cold River."

This was naturally a joke she said out of humility, but we can fully see how interested and hardworking she is in acting.

Film Novel

Little Minister (2) 221

— Zhi

The banquet was extremely dull, and she was unwilling to listen to their conversations. But when they talked about recent events in the village, she became attentive. Recently, some manufacturers had bought a large number of spinning machines, which had driven down the price of cloth in the market. Babaina knew that the poor people who depended on spinning for a living would suffer severely. They were considering using the army to suppress them. The captain was trying to capture their leader. At that moment, the duke said, "Yes, but they are not easy to deal with. I know they are all prepared." The captain, after downing a glass of wine, said with a smile, "Ha! Prepared." At that moment, he felt really pleased because Babaina kept asking him about this matter, but if he had known Babaina's true intentions, he certainly wouldn't have been so happy.

Babaina had a good friend who was the only constable in this area. She was often with him, but tonight she particularly wanted to talk to him. She asked, "If the army comes tonight, will you still be here?" "The army? Originally, my heart was with those spinners, but my duty is what it is, and there's nothing I can do. Now, if three bugle calls are sounded, they will all come." "Three bugle calls?" she asked. "That's their secret signal hidden in the Artersha factory. No one else knows it."

Babaina left immediately, running as fast as a real gypsy girl, because the army was set to move at midnight. As she was running, she heard footsteps behind her, and she wanted to hide, but it was too late. She said with a gypsy accent, "Sir, where is the road to Shana? I've lost my way." It was the little minister. Seeing her distraught appearance, dressed in gypsy clothes, with beautiful curls of hair and dreamy eyes, he said, "Perhaps I can help you." "Ah, sir, please tell me where the Artersha factory is? I need to see my father." Juemin believed her and said, "I'm passing by there too, I'll take you."

They proceeded in silence. She felt there was something special about him. He and his mother had come here as ministers. Soon after arriving, he became friendly with the villagers. Originally, it was very difficult for villagers and outsiders to get along in a short period of time.

On the way, Babaina started talking. "I think you must be the little minister people are talking about." "I am the new minister here. They say 'little' minister?" "No, I misspoke, but it wasn't meant to offend you. I actually like your stature." She kept talking. She knew he must be wondering whether, as a minister, he should be walking with a gypsy girl. Finally, she asked, "They say you are against the conflict between the textile workers and the army." Juemin answered in a tone reminiscent of the Bible, "I am against conflict. This is the yarn factory."

As soon as Babaina ran inside, she saw the big bugle. But she couldn't blow it. She ran out again and said to the little minister, "Sir, they've all run away, this bugle is for calling people. They must have left it here for me. Please blow it for me, will you?" Juemin blew the heavy bugle for a long time. Babaina said again, "This bugle is very hard to blow, I don't think you can blow it any louder." Juemin blew the bugle loudly again. Babaina clapped her hands happily and said, "Please blow it again." So he blew it once more. After the three calls were completed, the village erupted in shouts and drumbeats, and the army and the villagers began to fight.

At that moment, Juemin really didn't understand what was happening. Then she was about to run away. Her parting kiss left the little minister bewildered. She smiled at him and said, "Mr. Juemin, I believe you have always liked me. Can a man stop himself from liking a woman?" He said goodnight to each other and left. Babaina returned to the village, no longer thinking about the minister. She knew he was different. He was going to obey the law, while she was going to lead the villagers to resist the army. (To be continued)

Shanghai News Local Supplement - Automobile Weekly

Knowledge Needed When Buying a Car 222

— Junshan

Among hundreds of car manufacturers and hundreds of styles, choosing a suitable and economical car is not an easy problem to solve.

Whether buying a new car is appropriate depends on individual needs. Most unbiased buyers tend to let the salesman's silver tongue decide their choice. Therefore, in addition to continuously improving their products, car manufacturers are pushing their sales efforts to the extreme. To avoid being deceived by sweet talk and to hope to get a truly economical and suitable new car, reading what is described in this article will be helpful.

Cylinders and Fuel: The engine is the main part of a car. The usual numbers are two, four, six, eight, twelve, and sixteen cylinders. Generally, cars with more cylinders have more perfect body equipment and are more expensive. The power generated by each engine is based on the size of the bore, and the strength is not absolutely determined by the number of cylinders. In terms of comfort, more engine cylinders provide a more comfortable ride. For engines with the same horsepower, those with more cylinders consume more gasoline than those with fewer. Although gasoline seems like a small expense, when calculated across the board, the value consumed over two or three years can be equal to the cost of a new car. Wealthy people are willing to pay for further comfort without being concerned about this cost, but ordinary car owners may be very particular about it. If you are in the inland, where transportation is inconvenient and transportation is difficult, you should especially prioritize saving gasoline.

Choosing Horsepower: Choosing horsepower depends on the owner's use and road conditions. Too much or too little can cause the owner to suffer uneconomical losses. If the car owner intends to use the car to carry one or two people for office commuting, with a lighter load, they should choose a car with less horsepower. If the car is used by a salesperson who often carries goods and more people, it is best to choose a car with more horsepower. The quality of the road is also closely related to the need for horsepower. The horsepower required for cars traveling on flat and rugged mountain roads can differ by several or even dozens of times.

Determining Speed: Car manufacturers often specify a "standard speed" for speed, which varies from thirty, forty, to fifty miles per hour (some specially made vehicles have speeds exceeding seventy miles per hour). In detail, it means that the engine crankshaft rotates at one thousand, one thousand five, or two thousand revolutions per minute. Driving vehicles at this speed is most legal. Exceeding this number can easily damage the engine, and falling below this number is not economical in terms of fuel consumption. Road construction in my country is not yet developed, so the lowest standard speed is more suitable.

Electrical System Equipment: Although the principles of car electrical systems are the same, the devices are different. The strength of the lights, the loudness of the horn, and the important ignition equipment should be carefully considered and properly selected. Most American-made cars use battery ignition, while European-made cars have both battery and magneto ignition, as well as battery ignition. If the car you buy is used in commercial ports, all of the above ignition methods can be applied. If you are in a remote city with no battery charging facility, once the battery runs out of power, the engine cannot be started. At that time, it will inevitably be stranded, which is very troublesome. Therefore, cars used in the interior should preferably have magneto ignition.

Maintenance and Repair: Paying attention to the engine's efficiency and the ease with which diseases occur is the first priority when buying a car. Even those who are proficient in this area cannot easily have a definitive guarantee on this issue. Because the disease of a car depends entirely on the quality of maintenance and repair, and only a very small part is due to the manufacturer's rough inspection. In terms of the car itself, the more valuable the car, the more sophisticated the equipment and the longer the service life. Cheaper cars have simpler equipment and a shorter service life. The simplicity or complexity of maintenance and repair also varies greatly from car to car. For the average car owner, before buying, you should know a little about the structure of the internal organization, so that you can be more confident. Otherwise, in addition to comparing goods and prices, you should choose those that are simple in design and easy to maintain and repair. Because easy maintenance can reduce diseases, and easy repair can save money and time. Both are in line with economic conditions.

Body Style: The style of the body is like our clothing, and should be chosen according to personal preferences and needs. There are many types of bodies. The common ones are convertible cars, sedans, convertible roadsters, sedan roadsters, luxurious large sedans, etc. Convertible cars and sedans have five or seven seats, which are suitable for large families and for carrying a large number of people. The larger the body, the greater the load, so the consumption of gasoline is particularly high, and the engine's load is also heavy. Its service life is also relatively short. Convertible car bodies are simple to manufacture and cheap to sell, making them especially suitable for tropical regions and economical car owners. Sedan car bodies are complex to manufacture and expensive to sell, making them especially suitable for cold regions and people with ample economic means. Roadsters are also called office cars, and come in convertible and sedan styles. Because the body is light and small, gasoline is saved, and the engine's lifespan is also longer. But it can only carry one or two people, making it suitable for going to and from the office. There is a storage box in the back for carrying light items. If it is used for rental purposes, it is best to purchase luxurious large sedans and special rental-style convertible sedans.

Parts and Equipment: Before planning to buy a car, you should first ask yourself whether there is a dealership and service department for that car nearby and what the service is like. Are parts always available and what is the price of parts? The value of repairing and replacing parts for a car over three to five years is often equal to the original price of the car. It is inevitable that cars will be damaged after being used for a long time. After the damage, if there are no specialized skilled workers to repair it or if parts cannot be obtained, you will inevitably have to go to a coppersmith to have them made in the same way. These custom-made parts are always several times more expensive than ordinary ones, and their effectiveness is also lacking. The reason why Ford and Chevrolet cars have the widest sales is because the parts are cheap and easy to obtain.

Market Conditions: Before buying, you should also investigate the reputation and trading conditions of a certain car on the market. According to social judgment, some cars have a resale value that is almost the same as their original purchase price within one or two years of new use, while other cars have a greatly reduced resale value or are completely unwanted after being used for one or two years. Economical car owners should pay attention to this market demand situation.

Marius's Standard Testing Machine 224

— Fu

How much the finest automotive body materials are affected by light can now be accurately determined. A machine is now installed in the Marius Motor Company's testing room, which can make the impact of light on materials in 64 hours equal to the impact of a full year of strong summer sunlight.

Thus, in two and a half days, chemists can determine whether a sample material meets the specified standards. If the results are deemed satisfactory, another test is performed on the sample and the sample of the goods received. For example, the elasticity of the material used for carpets and the extent to which it can withstand the stepping of drivers and passengers must meet the standards. To know whether it meets the standards, you only need to use the machine to make it receive the same impact as stepping in a very short time, which is equal to the actual application for several months. Because Marius has this kind of machine, all the materials it uses are unusually fine and consistent with its noble standards.
