New Contribution of Dodge Motor Company 225

—

Building the Most Perfect Tuberculosis X-ray Mobile Treatment Vehicle

Dodge Motor Company, under the order of the Public Health Department of the Department of Health and Medical Affairs, has built a tuberculosis X-ray treatment vehicle for mobile diagnosis. The chassis of this special vehicle is a Dodge 11/2-ton (240Cwt) model. The construction method is completely in accordance with the regulations of the department. The car body is divided into two sections except for the driving part. The rear compartment is where patients enter the vehicle, named the laboratory, occupying a five-foot space at the rear of the car body. All drug materials are stored in specially made medicine cabinets and drawers in this section of the car. In addition, there is a washing basin and a 30-gallon water tank to supply various hygiene needs and to wash X-ray photos. This section of the car is painted white and black linoleum is laid on the bottom plate.

The X-ray room is located in front of the laboratory, occupying a ten-foot space. There is a door between the two rooms that can be connected. All X-ray equipment and beds for patients to take photos are complete. The X-ray tube is flexible, so any part of the body can be inspected or photographed. Film storage boxes and washing basins are also available in the X-ray room. Once the steel curtain is lowered, the car windows are completely covered. Then the department can become a darkroom. The interior of this section of the car is painted black and black linoleum is laid on the bottom plate. The X-ray room is equipped with four 15-candlepower lamps and a motor-driven ventilation fan to ensure that the air in both sections of the car is well ventilated. The X-ray is powered by electricity, which is supplied by a special generator.

This mobile clinic is the most modern and perfect of its kind ever built. Since its completion, the medical and scientific communities have paid close attention and praised it.

Road Construction News from Henan and Gansu Provinces 226

— Yang Dehui

In recent years, Henan Province has enjoyed local peace and stability, leading to a strong interest in construction projects. In particular, there has been rapid progress in highway construction. I will now inform readers about the construction of highways in Henan and Gansu provinces.

(1) Luotong Road: Starting from Luoyang, passing through Yiyang, Luoning, Lushi, Wenxiang, and other counties to Tongguan, it is 330 kilometers long. Construction has already begun on the Luoyang to Luoning section. The survey of the Luoning to Lushi County section has been completed. The Lushi to Wenxiang section has also been surveyed. The engineering team is currently building the roadbed for the Wenxiang to Tongguan section. (2) Lulin Road: From Luoyang to Linru, it is 85.8 kilometers long. The survey has been completed and construction is underway. (3) Zhouhuang Road: From Zhoukou to Huangchuan, it is 177.2 kilometers long. The road surface construction was completed in June. Bridge and culvert construction along the route is actively progressing and will soon be completed and open to traffic. (4) Nanxiang Road: Starting from Nanyang, passing through Xinye and Deng County to Xiangfan in Hubei Province. The road surface construction within the provincial border has been completed. The massive bridge project across the Baihe River is still under inspection. (5) Xinjing Road: From Xinyang to Zijingguan, it is 352.9 kilometers long, passing through Tongbai, Tanghe, Xinye, Zheng County, Zhechuan, and other counties. The survey has been completed and construction will begin once the funding is approved. (6) Shajing Road: From Shawo to Jingfu County, it is 25.52 kilometers long. Construction has already begun and it will soon be completed and open to traffic. (7) Xunan Road: From Xuchang to Nanyang, the roadbed earthwork for the entire road has been completed. The construction of bridges and culverts along the route is being supervised by the Construction Department and has begun in various counties. (wty, Lujing Road: From Lushi County, passing through Zhuyangguan to Zijingguan) is approximately 70 kilometers long. A survey has been conducted and construction is planned. Fanghuang Road: From Xiaofangjiaji to Huangtouling, it is 18.9 kilometers long. The earthwork for the entire road has been completed. It will be open to traffic once the bridges are completed.

Gansu Province suffers from poor transportation, which has led to the backwardness of industry and commerce. The provincial government, with the aim of actively promoting construction, focuses on highways. Therefore, it has formulated a provincial highway plan, which includes: (1) Ganling Road: Starting from Gaolan, passing through Yuzhong, Dingxi, Jingning, Longde, Pingliang, Jingchuan to Yaodian, it is 572 kilometers long and is an important route to Shaanxi. It is also known as the Gansu-Shaanxi trunk line and can connect with the Changwu Road in Shaanxi. This road was originally named Lanzhai Road. Although it has been repaired over the years, due to financial constraints, surveying has never been carried out. The estimated construction cost is 986,414,000 yuan. (2) Ganxin Line: Starting from Gaolan, passing through Yongdeng, Gulang, Wuwei, Yongchang, Shandan, Zhangye, Linze, Gaotai, Jiuquan, Yumen, Anxi to Xingxing Gorge, it is 1,481 kilometers long. The terrain along the route is quite diverse. Crossing the Jincheng Pass west of Fulan City and traveling west along the coast for about ten miles, it enters the mountains. Therefore, the project is quite grand. The estimated cost is 2,553,984,000 yuan. This road connects to Hami in Xinjiang and is also a section of the national Fujian-Xinjiang line. (3) Ganqing Line: Starting from Gaolan to Xiangtang, directly reaching Xining, it is 185 kilometers long. If traveling from Gansu to Tibet, this route is followed. It is extremely important in terms of politics and national defense. There are several cliffs along the route that overhang the river, making the project relatively large. The estimated construction cost is 319,032,500 yuan. (4) Ganning Line: Starting northeast from Gaolan, passing through Jingyuan to Xingrenpu and entering Ningxia, it is 237 kilometers long. If extended, it can reach Baotou, connecting with the northeastern provinces, making transportation quite important. The estimated cost is 408,706,500 yuan. (5) The First Gansu-Sichuan Line: Starting from Gaolan, along the Mengjiapu of the Gansu-Shaanxi Line, passing through Tongwei, Qin'an, Tianshui, Liangdang, Huixian, Cheng County, Wudu, Bikou to Chengdu in Sichuan Province, it is 854 kilometers long. The section from Huajialing to Tianshui already has a road shape and can be repaired. The area south of Tianshui is mostly a horse trail. The estimated construction cost is 1,472,723,000 yuan. (6) The Second Gansu-Sichuan Line: Starting from Gaolan, passing through Tao Sha, Lintan, Minxian, Xigu, Wudu to Bikou, it is 622 kilometers long. The estimated construction cost is 1,072,639,000 yuan. The first and second Gansu-Sichuan lines connect the wealthy areas of southern Gansu, control Sichuan to the south, and rely on Guanzhong to the west, making the geographical location very important. Of the above six major trunk lines, only the roads from Lanzhou to Xi'an, Xining, and Ningxia can barely be opened to traffic according to the old roads. However, all require fundamental construction. These six lines total 3,951 kilometers in length. The total estimated construction cost is 6,813,499.50 yuan. This is still a temporary estimate for bridges along the route. If semi-permanent structures are adopted and the excavated areas are widened to double-lane roads, the estimated construction cost will increase. If using semi-permanent brick and stone piers with wooden surfaces for bridges, the average cost is 420 yuan per meter, and approximately 2,100 yuan per kilometer, assuming five meters per kilometer. For special bridges with spans of more than five meters, semi-permanent structures are also planned, with an average cost of 450 yuan per meter, and approximately 150 yuan per kilometer, assuming one-third of a meter per kilometer. The average cost of stonework is estimated at 50 cubic meters per kilometer, with each cubic meter costing approximately 1.50 yuan, totaling approximately 75 yuan. Considering these costs, as well as labor and other expenses, the six major lines will total 13,026,447 yuan, more than double the previously estimated cost. The provincial government is currently gradually studying the steps for phased construction to facilitate development.

Overseas Automotive News 227

— Zhenmin

Ford Company's Losses Last Year: According to a recent report by Mr. Kamolong, secretary of Ford Motor Company, on the radio in the United States, the most notable thing is that the company's operating loss last year reached US$68,000,000. This news caused great shock to American women. Ford Motor Company is the largest automobile factory in the United States. Its manufacturing steps and management methods all adopt the latest and most scientific systems. The current result is quite unexpected. Henry Ford himself stated that the biggest reason for last year's losses was the rapid change in car body styles. Some cars experienced sluggish sales. In addition, last year's increase in workers' wages and other expenses remained unchanged, failing to offset each other. However, Ford's intention is quite firm, saying that this loss is just a very small experiment and has no impact on the overall situation. It is expected that this year's income will definitely make up for this loss.

German Auto Show Under Hitler's Command: Recently, Germany held a grand auto show that had not been seen for several years. Marshal Hitler personally attended the opening ceremony, which made the venue even more enthusiastic. German newspapers promoted the event as the world's largest auto show. In total, in this exhibition, except for a small number of American cars from Ford's branch, all other cars were purely German-made. A total of sixteen car factories participated, with more than fifty new types of cars. The most satisfying thing in the exhibition was the exquisite and compact engine manufacturing, with extremely high efficiency. The metal of the cylinder is a newly invented aluminum alloy, which can avoid rust and other phenomena, while increasing strength and promoting a very high compression ratio. Secondly, the progress of streamlining is also very significant. The material of the car body has almost completely adopted all-steel sheets, which are lightweight, durable, and very special. According to the interim report on operating conditions, Vnion had the best sales last year, and Dgimler was a little worse, but all factories had very substantial surpluses.
